function checkJota(int) {

    var jotaObject = {};
    digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function(el) {
        var jota = el.backendCategory.slice(0, int);
        if (jotaObject[jota] === undefined) {
            jotaObject[jota] = el.price * el.quantity;
        } else {
            jotaObject[jota] = jotaObject[jota] + (el.price * el.quantity);
        }
    });

    var finalJota;
    Object.keys(jotaObject).forEach(function(el) {
        if (finalJota === undefined) {
            finalJota = el;
        } else {
 
            finalJota = jotaObject[finalJota] > jotaObject[el] ? finalJota : el;

        }

    });
    return finalJota;

}

function getProd() {
	var prodsArr = []
	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {
		var tempObj = {
			'sku': el.sku,
			'price': el.price,
			'quantity': el.quantity
		};
		prodsArr.push(tempObj);
	});
	return prodsArr;
}

function getTotal() {
	var total = 0;
	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {
		total = el.price + total;
	})
	return total;
}
